<div class="comment-renderer-content"><div class="comment-renderer-header"><a href="/user/newstart7000" class="comment-author-text yt-uix-sessionlink      spf-link " data-sessionlink="itct=CFsQtnUiEwiZ-5Kdwa_dAhUZ3cEKHcVtAl8">Pickel Sandwich</a><span class="comment-renderer-time" tabindex="0"><a href="/watch?v=8KkKuTCFvzI&amp;lc=UgzwVYfFhw0QUWxm-CR4AaABAg" class="yt-uix-sessionlink       spf-link " data-sessionlink="itct=CFsQtnUiEwiZ-5Kdwa_dAhUZ3cEKHcVtAl8">il y a 2&nbsp;mois (modifié)</a></span></div><div class="comment-renderer-text" tabindex="0" role="article"><div class="comment-renderer-text-content">I am 60 and now, looking back, I realize something.   I have done more in my life than most people I have met in life,  friends and family.   I have almost always done what I wanted to do.  Most people I have met over the years have not ! I was never afraid.&#65279;</div><div class="comment-text-toggle"><div class="comment-text-toggle-link read-more"><button class="yt-uix-button yt-uix-button-size-default yt-uix-button-link" type="button" onclick="return false;"><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Lire la suite
